#Nation individual flagsetting events by Killerrabbit
#All nations will have these, which is a prerequsite for Scud's economic events to function.
#
#The modifiers are simulating the level of corruption in the country + Defence budget and Free Marked - Planned Economy settings.
#
#

event = {
	id = 233000
	persistent = no
	random = no
	country = ALB
